  <div id="mainview">
      <div id="mission">
          <div class="buildingDescription">
              <h1>Pilhar</h1>
              <p>As outras cidades podem ter tesouros que ficam melhor nos nossos armazéns. Mas lembra-te que as unidades custam mais manutenção se tiverem numa missão. Pensa duas vezes antes de enviar as tuas unidades para roubar.</p>

          <script type="text/javascript">
  
                          function missionController(freeTrans, transporterCapacity, transportJourneyTime, usedCapacity, missionTime,
                                         minimumJourneyDuration, isForeignIsland) {
                  var that = this;
                  this.unitsOk = false;
                  this.transportersOk = false;
                  this.registeredSliders = [];
  
                  this.extraTransporterEl = $("#extraTransporter")[0];
                  this.transporterCountEl = $("#transporterCount")[0];
                  this.freightEl = $("#totalFreight")[0];
                  this.journeyTimeEl = $('#journeyTime')[0];
                  this.returnTimeEl = $('#returnTime')[0];
                  this.upkeepEl = $('#upkeepPerHour')[0];
                  this.totalCostsEl = $('#estimatedTotalCosts')[0];
                  this.weightEl = $('#totalWeight')[0];
  
                  this.usedCapacity = usedCapacity;
                  this.freeTrans = freeTrans;
                  this.transporterCapacity = transporterCapacity;
                  this.totalCapacity = freeTrans * transporterCapacity;
                  this.transportJourneyTime = transportJourneyTime;
                  this.journeyTime = 0;
                  this.journeyTimeWithoutTransporters = 0;
                  this.sumTransporter = 0;
                  this.extraTransporter = 0;
                  this.missionTime = missionTime;
                  this.weight = 0;
                  this.disableChanged = 0;
                  this.transporterInput = false;
                  this.minimumJourneyDuration = minimumJourneyDuration;
                  this.isForeignIsland = isForeignIsland;
  
                  this.registerSlider = function (s) {
                      that.registeredSliders.push(s);
                      s.adjustSliderRange((s.weight === 0) ? s.maxValue : Math.min(s.maxValue, Math.floor((that.totalCapacity * that.freeTrans - (that.usedCapacity - s.actualValue * s.weight) ) / (s.weight))));
                      that.usedCapacity += s.actualValue * s.weight;
                      s.subscribe("valueChange", that.sliderChanged);
                      if (s.weight > 0) {
                          // Seems silly to call sliderEnd here but...
                          // it calculates the maxLoad ahead of time, not having to wait until the slider is first changed
                          that.sliderEnd();
                          s.subscribe("valueChange", that.sliderEnd);
                      }
                  };
  
                  this.setTransporterInput = function (transporterInput) {
                      this.transporterInput = transporterInput;
                  };
  
                  this.sliderEnd = function () {
                      if (that.disableChanged == false) {
                          that.disableChanged = true;
                          for (var i = 0; i < that.registeredSliders.length; i++) {
                              var s = that.registeredSliders[i];
                              var maxLoad = Math.min(s.maxValue, Math.floor((that.totalCapacity - (that.usedCapacity - s.actualValue * s.weight) ) / (s.weight)));
                              s.adjustSliderRange(maxLoad);
                          }
                          that.disableChanged = false;
                      }
                  };
  
                  this.sliderChanged = function () {
                      var tempUsedCapacity = 0;
                      var tempJourneyTime = 0;
                      var tempTransporterCount = 0;
                      var tempExtraTransporterCount = 0;
                      var totalUpkeep = 0;
                      var totalWeight = 0;
                      var tempUnitsOk = false;
  
                      var sliderLen = that.registeredSliders.length;
  
                      for (var i = 0; i < sliderLen; i++) {
                          tempUsedCapacity += (that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue * that.registeredSliders[i].weight);
                          if (that.registeredSliders[i].unitJourneyTime > tempJourneyTime && that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue > 0) {
                              tempJourneyTime = that.registeredSliders[i].unitJourneyTime;
                          }
                          totalUpkeep += that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue * that.registeredSliders[i].upkeep * 1;
                          totalWeight += that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue * that.registeredSliders[i].weight;
                          if (that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue > 0) {
                              tempUnitsOk = true;
                          }
                      }
                      that.journeyTimeWithoutTransporters = tempJourneyTime;
  
                      tempTransporterCount = Math.ceil(tempUsedCapacity / that.transporterCapacity);
                      if (that.extraTransporterEl !== undefined) {
                          tempExtraTransporterCount = that.extraTransporter;
                      } else {
                          tempExtraTransporterCount = 0;
                      }
                      if (tempTransporterCount + tempExtraTransporterCount > that.freeTrans) {
                          tempExtraTransporterCount = that.freeTrans - tempTransporterCount;
                          if (tempExtraTransporterCount < 0) tempExtraTransporterCount = 0;
                      }
                      if (tempTransporterCount > 0  && that.isForeignIsland || tempExtraTransporterCount > 0)  {
                          tempJourneyTime = Math.max(that.transportJourneyTime, tempJourneyTime);
                      }
  
                      that.updateSummary(
                          tempJourneyTime,
                          that.isForeignIsland ? tempTransporterCount : 0,
                          tempExtraTransporterCount,
                          Math.round(totalWeight),
                          Math.round(totalUpkeep),
                          tempUsedCapacity,
                          tempUnitsOk,
                          null,
                          null
                      );
                  };
  
                  this.missionTimeChanged = function (newTime) {
                      that.updateSummary(null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, parseInt(newTime));
                  };
  
                  this.updateSummary = function (journeyTime, sumTransporter, extraTransporter, weight, upkeep, capacity, unitsOk, transportersOkay, missionTime) {
                      if (capacity !== null) that.usedCapacity = capacity;
                      if (extraTransporter !== null) that.extraTransporter = extraTransporter;
                      if (sumTransporter !== null) that.sumTransporter = sumTransporter;
                      if (missionTime !== null) that.missionTime = missionTime;
                      if (transportersOkay !== null) {
                          that.transportersOk = transportersOkay;  // no transporters needed
                      }
                      if (unitsOk !== null) that.unitsOk = unitsOk;  // no slider changes
                      if (weight !== null && that.weightEl !== undefined) that.weight = weight;
  
                      if (that.transporterCountEl !== undefined) {
                          that.transporterCountEl.innerHTML = that.sumTransporter;
                      }
                      if (that.extraTransporterEl !== undefined) that.extraTransporterEl.value = that.extraTransporter;
  
                      if (journeyTime !== null) {
                          if (typeof journeyTime === "number"
                              && journeyTime > 0 && journeyTime < that.minimumJourneyDuration) {
                              journeyTime = that.minimumJourneyDuration;
                          }

  <div id="mainview">
      <div id="mission">
          <div class="buildingDescription">
              <h1>Estacionar frotas</h1>
              <p>Podes mover as tuas frotas de uma cidade para outra. Desta forma, é possível reforçar a tua própria frota ou ajudar frotas aliadas. Lembre-te que a frota fora do seu próprio porto a manutenção tem custos mais elevados.</p>

          <script type="text/javascript">
  
                          function missionController(freeTrans, transporterCapacity, transportJourneyTime, usedCapacity, missionTime,
                                         minimumJourneyDuration, isForeignIsland) {
                  var that = this;
                  this.unitsOk = false;
                  this.transportersOk = false;
                  this.registeredSliders = [];
  
                  this.extraTransporterEl = $("#extraTransporter")[0];
                  this.transporterCountEl = $("#transporterCount")[0];
                  this.freightEl = $("#totalFreight")[0];
                  this.journeyTimeEl = $('#journeyTime')[0];
                  this.returnTimeEl = $('#returnTime')[0];
                  this.upkeepEl = $('#upkeepPerHour')[0];
                  this.totalCostsEl = $('#estimatedTotalCosts')[0];
                  this.weightEl = $('#totalWeight')[0];
  
                  this.usedCapacity = usedCapacity;
                  this.freeTrans = freeTrans;
                  this.transporterCapacity = transporterCapacity;
                  this.totalCapacity = freeTrans * transporterCapacity;
                  this.transportJourneyTime = transportJourneyTime;
                  this.journeyTime = 0;
                  this.journeyTimeWithoutTransporters = 0;
                  this.sumTransporter = 0;
                  this.extraTransporter = 0;
                  this.missionTime = missionTime;
                  this.weight = 0;
                  this.disableChanged = 0;
                  this.transporterInput = false;
                  this.minimumJourneyDuration = minimumJourneyDuration;
                  this.isForeignIsland = isForeignIsland;
  
                  this.registerSlider = function (s) {
                      that.registeredSliders.push(s);
                      s.adjustSliderRange((s.weight === 0) ? s.maxValue : Math.min(s.maxValue, Math.floor((that.totalCapacity * that.freeTrans - (that.usedCapacity - s.actualValue * s.weight) ) / (s.weight))));
                      that.usedCapacity += s.actualValue * s.weight;
                      s.subscribe("valueChange", that.sliderChanged);
                      if (s.weight > 0) {
                          // Seems silly to call sliderEnd here but...
                          // it calculates the maxLoad ahead of time, not having to wait until the slider is first changed
                          that.sliderEnd();
                          s.subscribe("valueChange", that.sliderEnd);
                      }
                  };
  
                  this.setTransporterInput = function (transporterInput) {
                      this.transporterInput = transporterInput;
                  };
  
                  this.sliderEnd = function () {
                      if (that.disableChanged == false) {
                          that.disableChanged = true;
                          for (var i = 0; i < that.registeredSliders.length; i++) {
                              var s = that.registeredSliders[i];
                              var maxLoad = Math.min(s.maxValue, Math.floor((that.totalCapacity - (that.usedCapacity - s.actualValue * s.weight) ) / (s.weight)));
                              s.adjustSliderRange(maxLoad);
                          }
                          that.disableChanged = false;
                      }
                  };
  
                  this.sliderChanged = function () {
                      var tempUsedCapacity = 0;
                      var tempJourneyTime = 0;
                      var tempTransporterCount = 0;
                      var tempExtraTransporterCount = 0;
                      var totalUpkeep = 0;
                      var totalWeight = 0;
                      var tempUnitsOk = false;
  
                      var sliderLen = that.registeredSliders.length;
  
                      for (var i = 0; i < sliderLen; i++) {
                          tempUsedCapacity += (that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue * that.registeredSliders[i].weight);
                          if (that.registeredSliders[i].unitJourneyTime > tempJourneyTime && that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue > 0) {
                              tempJourneyTime = that.registeredSliders[i].unitJourneyTime;
                          }
                          totalUpkeep += that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue * that.registeredSliders[i].upkeep * 1;
                          totalWeight += that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue * that.registeredSliders[i].weight;
                          if (that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue > 0) {
                              tempUnitsOk = true;
                          }
                      }
                      that.journeyTimeWithoutTransporters = tempJourneyTime;
  
                      tempTransporterCount = Math.ceil(tempUsedCapacity / that.transporterCapacity);
                      if (that.extraTransporterEl !== undefined) {
                          tempExtraTransporterCount = that.extraTransporter;
                      } else {
                          tempExtraTransporterCount = 0;
                      }
                      if (tempTransporterCount + tempExtraTransporterCount > that.freeTrans) {
                          tempExtraTransporterCount = that.freeTrans - tempTransporterCount;
                          if (tempExtraTransporterCount < 0) tempExtraTransporterCount = 0;
                      }
                      if (tempTransporterCount > 0  && that.isForeignIsland || tempExtraTransporterCount > 0)  {
                          tempJourneyTime = Math.max(that.transportJourneyTime, tempJourneyTime);
                      }
  
                      that.updateSummary(
                          tempJourneyTime,
                          that.isForeignIsland ? tempTransporterCount : 0,
                          tempExtraTransporterCount,
                          Math.round(totalWeight),
                          Math.round(totalUpkeep),
                          tempUsedCapacity,
                          tempUnitsOk,
                          null,
                          null
                      );
                  };
  
                  this.missionTimeChanged = function (newTime) {
                      that.updateSummary(null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, parseInt(newTime));
                  };
  
                  this.updateSummary = function (journeyTime, sumTransporter, extraTransporter, weight, upkeep, capacity, unitsOk, transportersOkay, missionTime) {
                      if (capacity !== null) that.usedCapacity = capacity;
                      if (extraTransporter !== null) that.extraTransporter = extraTransporter;
                      if (sumTransporter !== null) that.sumTransporter = sumTransporter;
                      if (missionTime !== null) that.missionTime = missionTime;
                      if (transportersOkay !== null) {
                          that.transportersOk = transportersOkay;  // no transporters needed
                      }
                      if (unitsOk !== null) that.unitsOk = unitsOk;  // no slider changes
                      if (weight !== null && that.weightEl !== undefined) that.weight = weight;
  
                      if (that.transporterCountEl !== undefined) {
                          that.transporterCountEl.innerHTML = that.sumTransporter;
                      }
                      if (that.extraTransporterEl !== undefined) that.extraTransporterEl.value = that.extraTransporter;
  
                      if (journeyTime !== null) {
                          if (typeof journeyTime === "number"
                              && journeyTime > 0 && journeyTime < that.minimumJourneyDuration) {
                              journeyTime = that.minimumJourneyDuration;
                          }

                          function missionController(freeTrans, transporterCapacity, transportJourneyTime, usedCapacity, missionTime,
                                         minimumJourneyDuration, isForeignIsland) {
                  var that = this;
                  this.unitsOk = false;
                  this.transportersOk = false;
                  this.registeredSliders = [];
  
                  this.extraTransporterEl = $("#extraTransporter")[0];
                  this.transporterCountEl = $("#transporterCount")[0];
                  this.freightEl = $("#totalFreight")[0];
                  this.journeyTimeEl = $('#journeyTime')[0];
                  this.returnTimeEl = $('#returnTime')[0];
                  this.upkeepEl = $('#upkeepPerHour')[0];
                  this.totalCostsEl = $('#estimatedTotalCosts')[0];
                  this.weightEl = $('#totalWeight')[0];
  
                  this.usedCapacity = usedCapacity;
                  this.freeTrans = freeTrans;
                  this.transporterCapacity = transporterCapacity;
                  this.totalCapacity = freeTrans * transporterCapacity;
                  this.transportJourneyTime = transportJourneyTime;
                  this.journeyTime = 0;
                  this.journeyTimeWithoutTransporters = 0;
                  this.sumTransporter = 0;
                  this.extraTransporter = 0;
                  this.missionTime = missionTime;
                  this.weight = 0;
                  this.disableChanged = 0;
                  this.transporterInput = false;
                  this.minimumJourneyDuration = minimumJourneyDuration;
                  this.isForeignIsland = isForeignIsland;
  
                  this.registerSlider = function (s) {
                      that.registeredSliders.push(s);
                      s.adjustSliderRange((s.weight === 0) ? s.maxValue : Math.min(s.maxValue, Math.floor((that.totalCapacity * that.freeTrans - (that.usedCapacity - s.actualValue * s.weight) ) / (s.weight))));
                      that.usedCapacity += s.actualValue * s.weight;
                      s.subscribe("valueChange", that.sliderChanged);
                      if (s.weight > 0) {
                          // Seems silly to call sliderEnd here but...
                          // it calculates the maxLoad ahead of time, not having to wait until the slider is first changed
                          that.sliderEnd();
                          s.subscribe("valueChange", that.sliderEnd);
                      }
                  };
  
                  this.setTransporterInput = function (transporterInput) {
                      this.transporterInput = transporterInput;
                  };
  
                  this.sliderEnd = function () {
                      if (that.disableChanged == false) {
                          that.disableChanged = true;
                          for (var i = 0; i < that.registeredSliders.length; i++) {
                              var s = that.registeredSliders[i];
                              var maxLoad = Math.min(s.maxValue, Math.floor((that.totalCapacity - (that.usedCapacity - s.actualValue * s.weight) ) / (s.weight)));
                              s.adjustSliderRange(maxLoad);
                          }
                          that.disableChanged = false;
                      }
                  };
  
                  this.sliderChanged = function () {
                      var tempUsedCapacity = 0;
                      var tempJourneyTime = 0;
                      var tempTransporterCount = 0;
                      var tempExtraTransporterCount = 0;
                      var totalUpkeep = 0;
                      var totalWeight = 0;
                      var tempUnitsOk = false;
  
                      var sliderLen = that.registeredSliders.length;
  
                      for (var i = 0; i < sliderLen; i++) {
                          tempUsedCapacity += (that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue * that.registeredSliders[i].weight);
                          if (that.registeredSliders[i].unitJourneyTime > tempJourneyTime && that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue > 0) {
                              tempJourneyTime = that.registeredSliders[i].unitJourneyTime;
                          }
                          totalUpkeep += that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue * that.registeredSliders[i].upkeep * 1;
                          totalWeight += that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue * that.registeredSliders[i].weight;
                          if (that.registeredSliders[i].actualValue > 0) {
                              tempUnitsOk = true;
                          }
                      }
                      that.journeyTimeWithoutTransporters = tempJourneyTime;
  
                      tempTransporterCount = Math.ceil(tempUsedCapacity / that.transporterCapacity);
                      if (that.extraTransporterEl !== undefined) {
                          tempExtraTransporterCount = that.extraTransporter;
                      } else {
                          tempExtraTransporterCount = 0;
                      }
                      if (tempTransporterCount + tempExtraTransporterCount > that.freeTrans) {
                          tempExtraTransporterCount = that.freeTrans - tempTransporterCount;
                          if (tempExtraTransporterCount < 0) tempExtraTransporterCount = 0;
                      }
                      if (tempTransporterCount > 0  && that.isForeignIsland || tempExtraTransporterCount > 0)  {
                          tempJourneyTime = Math.max(that.transportJourneyTime, tempJourneyTime);
                      }
  
                      that.updateSummary(
                          tempJourneyTime,
                          that.isForeignIsland ? tempTransporterCount : 0,
                          tempExtraTransporterCount,
                          Math.round(totalWeight),
                          Math.round(totalUpkeep),
                          tempUsedCapacity,
                          tempUnitsOk,
                          null,
                          null
                      );
                  };
  
                  this.missionTimeChanged = function (newTime) {
                      that.updateSummary(null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, parseInt(newTime));
                  };
  
                  this.updateSummary = function (journeyTime, sumTransporter, extraTransporter, weight, upkeep, capacity, unitsOk, transportersOkay, missionTime) {
                      if (capacity !== null) that.usedCapacity = capacity;
                      if (extraTransporter !== null) that.extraTransporter = extraTransporter;
                      if (sumTransporter !== null) that.sumTransporter = sumTransporter;
                      if (missionTime !== null) that.missionTime = missionTime;
                      if (transportersOkay !== null) {
                          that.transportersOk = transportersOkay;  // no transporters needed
                      }
                      if (unitsOk !== null) that.unitsOk = unitsOk;  // no slider changes
                      if (weight !== null && that.weightEl !== undefined) that.weight = weight;
  
                      if (that.transporterCountEl !== undefined) {
                          that.transporterCountEl.innerHTML = that.sumTransporter;
                      }
                      if (that.extraTransporterEl !== undefined) that.extraTransporterEl.value = that.extraTransporter;
  
                      if (journeyTime !== null) {
                          if (typeof journeyTime === "number"
                              && journeyTime > 0 && journeyTime < that.minimumJourneyDuration) {
                              journeyTime = that.minimumJourneyDuration;
                          }

      function createAbortPopup(eventId, armyType) {
          let target = armyType === 'spy' ?
              '?action=Espionage&function=abortSpyTraining&cityId=6581&eid=' + eventId +
              '&actionRequest=5f4e34db5673b2ee18ee66442e73d405&position=1' :
              '?action=CityScreen&function=abortMilitaryConstruction&cityId=6581&actionRequest=5f4e34db5673b2ee18ee66442e73d405&position=1&eid=' + eventId + '&type=' + armyType;
  
          ikariam.createPopup("abortPopup", '',
              ['Tens certeza que queres cancelar a construção deste edifício? Perderás todos os recursos que investiste!',
                  target,
                  'Sim', 'Abortar'], 1);
      }
  
      function recruitmentSpeedUpCall() {
          var selectedValue = $('.js_reduceItemSelect').val();
          var inventory = [];
          if (parseInt(selectedValue) === 0 || !inventory[selectedValue]) {
              return;
          }
          var url = inventory[selectedValue]['activationUrl'];
          ajaxHandlerCall(url);
      }
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
  
      $(document).ready(function () {
          getCountdown({
              enddate: '1774444562',
              currentdate: '1774372271',
              startdate: '1773969382',
              el: 'unitBuildCountDown',
              timeoutAjaxRequest: '?view=' + ikariam.templateView.id +
                  "&cityId=6581&position=1",
              progressBar: '#unitBuildProgress'
          });
      });
  
      function createAbortPopup(eventId, armyType) {
          let target = armyType === 'spy' ?
              '?action=Espionage&function=abortSpyTraining&cityId=6581&eid=' + eventId +
              '&actionRequest=42b7818a8499adcfc1bdb8b95b9e0171&position=1' :
              '?action=CityScreen&function=abortMilitaryConstruction&cityId=6581&actionRequest=42b7818a8499adcfc1bdb8b95b9e0171&position=1&eid=' + eventId + '&type=' + armyType;
  
          ikariam.createPopup("abortPopup", '',
              ['Tens certeza que queres cancelar a construção deste edifício? Perderás todos os recursos que investiste!',
                  target,
                  'Sim', 'Abortar'], 1);
      }
  
      function recruitmentSpeedUpCall() {
          var selectedValue = $('.js_reduceItemSelect').val();
          var inventory = [];
          if (parseInt(selectedValue) === 0 || !inventory[selectedValue]) {
              return;
          }
          var url = inventory[selectedValue]['activationUrl'];
          ajaxHandlerCall(url);
      }
  </script>

      function createAbortPopup(eventId, armyType) {
          let target = armyType === 'spy' ?
              '?action=Espionage&function=abortSpyTraining&cityId=6581&eid=' + eventId +
              '&actionRequest=909beecb2fa82b7a3cfec4b5aa2beead&position=11' :
              '?action=CityScreen&function=abortMilitaryConstruction&cityId=6581&actionRequest=909beecb2fa82b7a3cfec4b5aa2beead&position=11&eid=' + eventId + '&type=' + armyType;
  
          ikariam.createPopup("abortPopup", '',
              ['Tens certeza que queres cancelar a construção deste edifício? Perderás todos os recursos que investiste!',
                  target,
                  'Sim', 'Abortar'], 1);
      }
  
      function recruitmentSpeedUpCall() {
          var selectedValue = $('.js_reduceItemSelect').val();
          var inventory = [];
          if (parseInt(selectedValue) === 0 || !inventory[selectedValue]) {
              return;
          }
          var url = inventory[selectedValue]['activationUrl'];
          ajaxHandlerCall(url);
      }
  </script>
